Tgtaps: Telegram Mini Apps (TMA) 24.09.2024 15:21:39

591√ó1280, 19.5 KB
We are exited to introduce the block for connecting users' TON wallets to your Telegram Mini Apps!

TON wallets can be used for:
- sending Airdrop or paying rewards to your users;
- connecting users to external resources (exchanges, platforms, games, etc.);
- verifying users identities within your apps;

To get users' TON wallets:
- export users data by navigating to "Settings" -> "Users" -> "Export in CSV";
- use our verifying API integration.

900√ó900, 50.0 KB
Broadcasts are now available in TgTaps apps!

To create a broadcast:
1) Go to your app's "Settings"
2) Open the "Broadcast" tab
3) Add a new message and click "Save"

Broadcast features:
- format text using HTML tags (<b>, <u>, <a>);
- display a "Join app" button to re-engage your audience;
- include links to external resources or commands below the message
